  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }

<div class='communityQuestion'>
<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/340389-is-this-worth-finishing-this-book">* Is this worth finishing? 

this book is sitting on my shelf and i cant bring myself to keep reading it.
i LOVED beautiful disaster but i kinda wish i didnt read this book bc it ruined everything i felt about Travis and Abby. The ending of beautiful disaster was the perfect ending to their relationship. So why keep going ? :\ Suddenly all the small loving gestures they share feel too..worn out.</a>
</div>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer747944563" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10265255732757792807"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385588046i/7180466._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED **<br/><br/><b><em>A Beautiful Wedding </em> was passionate, emotional, and a whole lot of fun. In this beautiful novella, Jamie McGuire reminded me once again why Travis Maddox is and always will be my favorite bad boy. </b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“A Maddox boy will take you all the way to the edge, but if you go with him, he’ll follow you anywhere…<br/><br/>And when a Maddox boy falls in love, he loves forever.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Even though it had been over a year since I read <em>Beautiful Disaster,</em> I reconnected with the characters ri</span>
  <span id="freeText10265255732757792807" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385588046i/7180466._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED **<br><br><b><em>A Beautiful Wedding </em> was passionate, emotional, and a whole lot of fun. In this beautiful novella, Jamie McGuire reminded me once again why Travis Maddox is and always will be my favorite bad boy. </b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“A Maddox boy will take you all the way to the edge, but if you go with him, he’ll follow you anywhere…<br><br>And when a Maddox boy falls in love, he loves forever.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Even though it had been over a year since I read <em>Beautiful Disaster,</em> I reconnected with the characters right from the start. Told in both Travis and Abby's point of views, this novella takes us through the excitement of their top secret Vegas wedding giving us a glimpse into one of the most special occasions of their lives. It was a beautiful and wonderful way to revisit characters who already had a special place in my heart.<br><br>My favorite thing about Travis and Abby has always been how strongly they <em>love</em> each other, how they're not afraid to show that love, and how what they each want most is each other's happiness. Everything you could ever want to know about their wedding is answered here --  where, when, why, how....<br><br>Their texts were adorable (<i>“I look ducking amazing.”</i>), that gorgeous letter totally made me cry (and the kiss after *clutches heart*), the ceremony had me smiling from ear to ear (you’re going to love what Travis says!), their wedding night was just perfect (*fans self*), the tattoo parlor was hilarious (seriously, LOL Travis!!), oh and don’t even get me started on the bachelor party (all I’m going to say is that I cannot wait for Trent’s book!) and at the end, we also got to see them a year later renewing their vows, but this time with all their friends and family present. It truly was beautiful!<br><br>If you're a fan of Travis and Abby, this novella is a must read! It was the perfect treat for fans of this series!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“By anyone’s standards, we were too young to get married, too unpredictable. How many times had we hurt one another along the way, screamed at each other one minute and fallen into bed together the next? But… I looked at him, resolute. He was mine, and I was his. If I knew anything at all, it was that only those two things mattered.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><em>Thank you for the publishers for sending me a copy to review. Release date: December 10, 2013.</em><br><br>****************************<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="10265255732757792807" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_777231832" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/777231832" />
    <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews"><img alt="Tough Critic Book Reviews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1345668583p2/5336035.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/777231832?book_show_action=true">Nov 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tough Critic Book Reviews" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews">Tough Critic Book Reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer777231832" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer715543006968105876"><b>And she ripped my closure off like a bandaid!! Son of a….</b><br/><br/>When <i>A Beautiful Wedding</i> showed up at my doorstep, my emotions seized. I was exited. I was thrilled. I was scared. I was indifferent. I was a whole lot of everything all at once. The only thing my eyes could see was CAUTION. Caution written in bright green neon letters….with glitter. <br/><br/>Why?….<br/><br/>Because I…am an addict, and the drug that is a <i>Beautiful Disaster</i> <b>is</b> my drug of choice. Just opening my package made my hands shake. The addiction all s</span>
  <span id="freeText715543006968105876" style="display:none"><b>And she ripped my closure off like a bandaid!! Son of a….</b><br /><br />When <i>A Beautiful Wedding</i> showed up at my doorstep, my emotions seized. I was exited. I was thrilled. I was scared. I was indifferent. I was a whole lot of everything all at once. The only thing my eyes could see was CAUTION. Caution written in bright green neon letters….with glitter. <br /><br />Why?….<br /><br />Because I…am an addict, and the drug that is a <i>Beautiful Disaster</i> <b>is</b> my drug of choice. Just opening my package made my hands shake. The addiction all started with a tattooed tongue. That damn tattooed tongue, and I couldn't get enough. To this day, <i>Beautiful Disaster</i> holds my record for the most re-reads ever. I read it from start to finish, and from finish to start. I partied with my favorite scenes, and shot up with my favorite intimate moments. I inhaled into my system everything that is Abby and Travis. I <i>needed</i> to get my fix; I was a user, and I used often. I wanted more. Hell, we all did.<br /><br />Then came <i>Walking Disaster</i>, and with that came my recovery. It was like a twelve step program for my addiction. It was my rehab. My therapy. Getting to experience a book for the first time, for a second time, was a stroke of literary genius. We got our more, but in a way that protected the integrity of the story along with everything we love about this series. We were able to get <i>more</i> without risking the perfection of <i>Beautiful Disaster</i> with a sequel. <br /><br />Instead, <i>Walking Disaster</i> gave me closure. It gave me...completeness, and after reading those words, "The End", I felt it. <br /><br />Now, sitting on my doorstep was frickin pandora's box. A line of literary cocaine begging to be snorted. What the hell was I suppose to do. Call a sponsor? Go to a meeting? Someone in my neighborhood's bound to have some mild (but effective) mood altering medication, right? <br /><br />Here's where I'd like to say that I was strong. And looking back, three seconds (and only one shot of tequila) before tearing open the pages was pretty damn strong. Especially when the name of Jamie McGuire is staring right at your face. I swear, even the font taunted me. <br /><br />I totally caved.<br /><br />When am I ever going to learn that Jamie McGuire is always right. She knows what I need even before I do. Yes, <i>Walking Disaster</i> put a bandaid over my Beautiful Disaster hole, but <i>A Beautiful Wedding</i> filled the hole. <i>This</i> is the end. <br /><br />It may have started off with me wanting to punch Abby in the face, but it ended with acceptance. Acceptance because I had to remember something that me, myself once said about this series. It is perfectly imperfect. This isn't a fairy tale, it never was. Abby and Travis are two jagged edge puzzle pieces that somehow perfectly fit together. They have both driven us mad from the start, why would we expect that to change now. This is fictional reality at its finest.<br /><br />Then there's Travis. His dialogue in this book was funny, sweet, sexy, hot. I think my eyes even had an orgasm! I loved everything from the bachelor party to the letter. Oh sweet Jesus the letter. There was so much beauty in the words that I literarily had chills. Especially when they came from Travis. <br /><br />In the end however, I was left with a few unanswered questions concerning Abby's secret. And to be honest, I'm not sure I liked learning what I did about her actions. However, I'm guessing my questions may have been answered if I had taken the time to read between the lines instead of devouring it like I did, but I pretty much shit out all self control when it comes to Jamie McGuire. I also noticed one small discrepancy in one of the scenes, but it is so small that I'm sure the ONLY reason I noticed it was because of the uncountable re-reads I did of <i>Beautiful Disaster</i>. The only reason I'm mentioning it is because I hope other readers don't piss out the haterade over MINOR details. Take your nit-pickers parade down another street and just enjoy the story. READ. ENJOY. LOVE.<br /><br />This is definitely one of my favorite series of all time and I am so blessed to have gotten MORE! If you haven't read <i>Beautiful Disaster</i> yet, first off, congratulations on coming out of your coma. Yay for you! It's a miracle. Second, READ THIS SERIES!<br /><br />If you already have, <i>A Beautiful Wedding</i> is NOT one to miss!<br /><br />READ ON!</span>
  <a data-text-id="715543006968105876" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4414511703508400698"><b>4 I ♥ Travis stars!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505954486i/23974800.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“The only thing I’m afraid of is a life without you, Pigeon.” <br/>“Then you have nothing to be afraid of. We’re forever.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><br/><i>A Beautiful Wedding</i> follows Abby and Travis from the moment they become engaged, until a year after the wedding. We get to see inside the proposal, their time in Vegas, the actual wedding, and some time after the wedding. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505954486i/23974801.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Travis Maddox is one of my original favorite book boyfriends and I will always have a special place for him. He is all kinds of ma</span>
  <span id="freeText4414511703508400698" style="display:none"><b>4 I ♥ Travis stars!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505954486i/23974800.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“The only thing I’m afraid of is a life without you, Pigeon.” <br>“Then you have nothing to be afraid of. We’re forever.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><i>A Beautiful Wedding</i> follows Abby and Travis from the moment they become engaged, until a year after the wedding. We get to see inside the proposal, their time in Vegas, the actual wedding, and some time after the wedding. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505954486i/23974801.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Travis Maddox is one of my original favorite book boyfriends and I will always have a special place for him. He is all kinds of male perfection. I will read anything with him in it so I jumped right on this! <br><br>Why not 5 stars??? Well, I’ll just say- WTH Abby? I get where she was coming from, I do. I was, however disappointed with the ‘reason’ she rushed to marry Trav. I know she loves him and just wants to protect him, but I really thought it was because she loved him so much, after the fire and facing death, she couldn’t imagine a life without him. I think that bit of information would have been better left out.<br><br>Overall, still a fantastic little novella. Made me swoon, made me smile and made me laugh! Loved the texting between Trav and Abby-<br><br><b>I miss u</b><br> <i>I miss u too</i> <br><b>T-minus one hour. U ready yet?</b><br> <i>Not yet. U?</i><br><b>Hells yes. I look ducking amazing. <div id="review_765931995" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/765931995" />
    <a title="Akanksha❤ Søren♰" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6165339-akanksha-s-ren"><img alt="Akanksha❤ Søren♰" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1580373674p2/6165339.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/765931995?book_show_action=true">Nov 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Akanksha❤ Søren♰" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Akanksha❤ Søren♰" href="/user/show/6165339-akanksha-s-ren">Akanksha❤ Søren♰</a>
      </span>

        rated it

<div id="review_772083690" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/772083690" />
    <a title="Rose" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3399699-rose"><img alt="Rose" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1386022874p2/3399699.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/772083690?book_show_action=true">Nov 23, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rose" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rose" href="/user/show/3399699-rose">Rose</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3399699-rose?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3399699-rose?shelf=drama">drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3399699-rose?shelf=multi-povs">multi-povs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3399699-rose?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3399699-rose?shelf=quick-read">quick-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3399699-rose?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3399699-rose?shelf=novella">novella</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer772083690" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5299440746766746319"><b>Initial reaction:</b> Decided that I'd go ahead and write a formal review of this. Yeah, I didn't expect to read this and there's a bit of a story that I'll tell when I write the full review. This was about what I expected it to be - a bit on the cheese side, had some offenses to offer to the table (misogyny chiefly, but even very few instances of casual racism...fun times, not.) But believe it or not, Travis was probably more tame in this narrative than he was in either Beautiful Disaster or Walkin</span>
  <span id="freeText5299440746766746319" style="display:none"><b>Initial reaction:</b> Decided that I'd go ahead and write a formal review of this. Yeah, I didn't expect to read this and there's a bit of a story that I'll tell when I write the full review. This was about what I expected it to be - a bit on the cheese side, had some offenses to offer to the table (misogyny chiefly, but even very few instances of casual racism...fun times, not.) But believe it or not, Travis was probably more tame in this narrative than he was in either Beautiful Disaster or Walking Disaster (didn't mean he lacked annoying points).<br /><br />Abby on the other hand...<br /><br />I'll talk about it in the full review. There's a bit to cover, but I'm going to have to rely on what I remember.<br /> <br /><b>Full review:</b><br /> <br />Earlier this year (2013), I read what I thought was the last of the "Beautiful" series - "Walking Disaster" and thought something along the lines of "Ugh, THAT'S IT! I'm done, I'm through, no more trying to follow Travis and Abby Maddox because I find them both to be epic insufferable. They're married, this series is finished. I'm not subjecting myself to this kind of fantastical train wreck fraught with misogyny, repetition of things already happened, and other offenses And that epilogue was the most Mary Sue wish fulfillment thing I've ever read. No more. Never again."<br /> <br />"Walking Disaster" was featured not long ago on my personal top 10 worst reads on my blog, actually dethroning "Beautiful Disaster" out of the top ten at #8 on the list. (I think "Beautiful Disaster" is still somewhere in the top 20 if I were to make such a list that long. But I digress.)<br /> <br />Fast forward a number of months later, I realize that the Beautiful series is, in fact, not over. There's a novella, it's about the shotgun wedding that Travis and Abby have in Vegas.<br /> <br />My first instinct was to run. But the funny thing about life is that you could say you will never touch another book in a series or by a particular author, and somehow it comes back to bite you in the bum when you actually end up in a shotgun scenario of your own where you do the complete opposite because you're drawn, in all places and spaces, within a bookstore.<br /> <br />Here's the story: my area has a lot of used bookstores and I was perusing them for good deals with the possibility of getting some gifts for people I love, and probably a good deal for myself if the price was right. I didn't expect to find a copy of "A Beautiful Wedding" in the Bargain Bin at one of these stores. For one, the book just came out the day before - the one I saw in the bin was in used, but good condition. It's a hardback book, you could probably put it on a coffee table. You could also read it in a single sitting (which is what I ended up doing).<br /> <br />But as I picked it up, I couldn't help but think "This is short...but do I really want to do this? I know this is a book that I probably will have problems with, but it's in my hands. I could technically read it at the table nearby."<br /> <br />One of the store attendants told me that someone just brought the book in that morning to sell, and as I flipped through it, really the only thing about it that was odd was a few scuffs with the cover and edge of the book on the outside.<br /> <br />I decided I might as well, because some might be curious to see where the story goes and I wondered what exactly happened at the wedding. It took me inside an hour to finish it, so really - this wasn't long at all, but designed with your usual whirlwind drama.<br /> <br />The story takes place after the fire in "Beautiful Disaster" - where Travis and Abby escape the devastation and on their way to Vegas to have a "shotgun" wedding. But this story purports to describe the "real" story behind their sudden decision to get married.<br /> <br /><b>Abby marries Travis under false pretenses.</b> I figure I might as well say that straightaway, because that's the major conflict (if you can call it one). If you're looking for plausibility as to why, probably not a good idea to try to look too hard into it because you either might start wincing at the terms or laughing because it's not...really possible. Maybe somewhere between that reaction if you're critical of it. Some fans of this series might even be sketchy with that reveal because they might think "OMG, WTF? Abby wanted to marry Travis for that? That's not my happy romantic ending! I thought she *really* wanted to marry him."<br /> <br />Yeah, no. Not at that time anyway. <br /> <br />Abby, filled with anxiety over the whole measure of things, decides to have the shotgun wedding in Vegas so that she can save Travis from getting arrested on behalf of the events of the fire. The guy that Travis fought ended up dead (So, yay? Travis is not only misogynistic, but he's also a loosely connected murderer because he knocked the guy out and no one got him out of the fire? Great! *gives two thumbs up then frowns and turns them down*) The latter reveal comes later, but I'm going to focus on the false terms for a moment.<br /> <br />Abby doesn't tell Travis that he might be suspect wanted for questioning in this whole...situation. Instead, she lies to him, wants to get married then, and the two hop on a plane ride straight to Vegas, complete with a fake Elvis. Abby's in a big, big rush to get this wedding overwith so that Travis can be cleared of any kind of wrongdoing, since the wedding is their coer. Travis's brother Trent texts Abby with updates about the situation to see if Travis can get cleared. There's a lot of plot holes and suspension of disbelief entailed in all this, and I had a difficult time believing it.<br /> <br />Even when Trent points out the stupidity of that plan, Abby's like "Don't tell me it's stupid." =_____=<br /> <br />Travis does suspect Abby's hiding something, but mostly he thinks she's on edge about the wedding and might get cold feet. He observes her at one point crying as she talks to Trent on the cell, but he doesn't know what's going on. In other measures, Travis is still his charming misogynistic self in some terms. He even considers an attractive Chinese girl and thinks (paraphrased) "If I were my old self and not with Abby, I would totally bang this chick." Yeah...nah, he hasn't changed at this point of the story. But maybe I wouldn't expect him to because of the timeline. At least the character's are consistent, but thinking about the events of the fire, there are some stretches in the timeline taken here.<br /> <br />Anyway, wedding details. Abby gets her dress, Travis hires an Elvis, the two say their vows in a chapel. Abby even receives a "beyond the grave" letter from Travis's mother. It's a pre-written letter to Travis's wife about her "special" boy and telling Abby in so many words to take care of him.<br /> <br />This will make me sound somewhat heartless, but I thought that was total cheese the way it was done. I know there are some terminally ill people who write letters intended for their sons and daughters, and that's heartfelt, I get that. But honestly, there's no way that Travis's mother would know how her son would turn out to be, and I wasn't getting the motivation for his mother to write to his wife here. It was just...the strawberry on the very forced portrait that we get of Abby and Travis being "meant to be" together. I think McGuire still struggles to establish character motivations and background in her writing, and it was evident in this and other factors through the work, so it didn't sell me.<br /> <br />There were some really dry sexy times written here, didn't really do much for the character intimacy. At one point, Travis asks her about why Abby was crying and talking on the phone at the boutique she bought her dress (she didn't see him watching, as they conveniently were around the same place). Abby easily fields off his inquiry with something else. The issue is never brought up again.<br /> <br />No, I'm not kidding. So Travis never knew that Abby...really lied about her reasons for marrying him so quickly.<br /> <br />Potential plot conflict point dropped for the sake of love.<br /> <br />Later on, Abby goes with Travis to get "Mrs. Maddox" tattooed on her back, and America shows up briefly in the scene to curse Abby out about having a *real* wedding. The narrative fastforwards about a year later some time after that to show Abby and Travis having a traditional wedding in the Carribean. Travis is noted around this time to have his anger issues under wraps because he "hasn't punched anybody" in a while according to Abby. Meh.<br /> <br />Kara makes a brief appearance in this book, as does Shep and some of the other characters, but they're more background noise for the story than anything else.<br /> <br />I think in the sum of things, there's problems peppered through this narrative that are technical in the suspension of disbelief for the turns of events. I took issue with the very few presentation of the characters of color here - what with the aforementioned Chinese girl and the presentation of a limo driver who addressed Travis as "Mistah Maddox", but then spoke without a dialect for the remaining phrase. The limo driver was never mentioned for race, but upon context clues...seriously? I don't know how to take that personally, and it made me want to facepalm more than a few times.<br /> <br />Overall, about what I expected for the novella. I take it fans probably won't care. Me, I'm just on my floating solitary cloud for not believing in the happily ever after. I've read more endearing stories that were just as short with more sweetness while not trying to shove the romance down my throat. *holds up umbrella*<br /> <br />At least the characterization was consistent, and Travis was considerably more tame in personality since his anger and antics were pulled back significantly. Not a true progressive reformation for the guy, and honestly, that could've been shown even more in this novella. Abby was more of the sketchy party here (and one could make an argument that there's some subtle female condescension in that). Travis ends up being the good guy, and she ends up being the...well, not honest one. And that was an opportunity missed to actually put forth some palpable conflict to deal with the honesty issue between them, but it just bulldozed its way to the happy ending without consequence.<br /> <br />In sum, short read, but still full of problems for what it offered.<br /> <br />Overall: 1/5 stars</span>
  <a data-text-id="5299440746766746319" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_748251591" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/748251591" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/748251591?book_show_action=true">Oct 24, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

          marked it as considering




        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer748251591" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10754292237182528247"><b>OHMYGOD!!!!!!!!!... OKAY so I'm not a huge fan of novellas, but it's Travis, so enough said.</b> TBR 12/10<br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/NYrv7OA' rel='nofollow noopener'>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1533908377" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer10210599659005480062"><u>4 Getting married! ★'s</u> <br/><br/><i>“A Maddox boy will take you all the way to the edge, but if you go with him, he’ll follow you anywhere…”</i><br/><br/>Thank you <i>Jamie McGuire</i> for giving us all what we so desperately needed!! This is a novella on ♥Abby and Travis’s♥ Las Vegas elopement :) It was amazing getting a look at how their wedding all went down and everything else in between! But the reason for Abby's decision to marry him kinda destroyed my heart. For Travis 😭. I mean really?? TWF... Whyyy did that have to be t</span>
  <span id="freeText10210599659005480062" style="display:none"><u>4 Getting married! ★'s</u> <br><br><i>“A Maddox boy will take you all the way to the edge, but if you go with him, he’ll follow you anywhere…”</i><br><br>Thank you <i>Jamie McGuire</i> for giving us all what we so desperately needed!! This is a novella on ♥Abby and Travis’s♥ Las Vegas elopement :) It was amazing getting a look at how their wedding all went down and everything else in between! But the reason for Abby's decision to marry him kinda destroyed my heart. For Travis 😭. I mean really?? TWF... Whyyy did that have to be the deciding factor behind it! I really wish that tidbit wasn't included. Other than that punch to my bleeding heart everything feels complete now :) And as always, anything that includes a Travis Maddox is always treasured and loved dearly. Travis was one of my very first book boyfriends, therefore he will always have a special place in my heart. Travis Travis Travis Travis!!! I love him so gosh damn much, I can't get enough. I'd seriously read anything with him in it!! ANYTHING. This was a wonderful short read that won't let you down. If you loved <i>Beautiful Disaster</i> and <i>Walking Disaster</i> as much as I do, you really won't want to miss out on this one. Oh the feels, just too many feels. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1533244170i/26068177._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>“I want you to know that whatever love is, this has got to be it. We were best friends first, and we tried not to fall in love, and we did anyway. If you’re not with me, it’s not where I want to be. I’m in this. I’m with you.” <br><br>“He was mine, and I was his. If I knew anything at all, it was that only those two things mattered.”</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1533272286ra/26069434.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>“I know you know I love you. What you may not know is that there is nothing I want more than to be your husband.”</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1533272286ra/26069435.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>“The only thing I'm afraid of is a life without you, Pigeon."<br>"Then you have nothing to be afraid of," I said. "We're forever.”</i><br><br><i>“And when a Maddox boy falls in love, he loves forever.”</i></span>

<div id="review_772753437" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/772753437" />
    <a title="Nasty Lady MJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4026143-nasty-lady-mj"><img alt="Nasty Lady MJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1506395877p2/4026143.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/772753437?book_show_action=true">Nov 24, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nasty Lady MJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nasty Lady MJ" href="/user/show/4026143-nasty-lady-mj">Nasty Lady MJ</a>
      </span>

          marked it as turnips



          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">People Who Like the Same Shitty Story</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Nasty Lady MJ by: </span>
      Hahaha No One
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer772753437" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer392661050952627561">Almost tempted to put this in my cash cow category (ca-ching), but since the series is so utterly horrible by itself it's being marked for this category. I will not read this. People who tell me that my review is mean, that I'm a bitch, or any of the usual crap will get laughed at and told to go away. <br/><br/>Now that the disclaimer is out of the way, here are my top ten reasons why I won't be reading this:<br/><br/><br/>10) I don't want to know what's going on in Abby's head. I already read her POV in Shitty Disaster</span>
  <span id="freeText392661050952627561" style="display:none">Almost tempted to put this in my cash cow category (ca-ching), but since the series is so utterly horrible by itself it's being marked for this category. I will not read this. People who tell me that my review is mean, that I'm a bitch, or any of the usual crap will get laughed at and told to go away. <br /><br />Now that the disclaimer is out of the way, here are my top ten reasons why I won't be reading this:<br /><br /><br />10) I don't want to know what's going on in Abby's head. I already read her POV in Shitty Disaster and know that it's probably nothing than oogling at Travis's hot bod.<br /><br />9) Besides everyone knows that most people only get married in Vegas if a) they're drunk, b) a celebrity, c) impulsive, d) trying to be hipster ironic, or e) live there. Most of the time these weddings are headed towards disaster though there are exceptions. Travis and Abby are NOT the exception despite what McGuire tried to convince us in that crapilouge of Shitty Disaster via Travis (better know as the epilogue where McGuire tells off naysayers).<br /><br />8) Wasn't the wedding already explained in Shitty Disaster?<br /><br />7) The fact I'll have to watch Travis commit several federal crimes at the airport and escape justice again would make me very sad.<br /><br />6) How is a wedding between two teenagers (well, one teen and an early twenty-something) a good thing? They can't support themselves, save for old Travis boy hitting someone and that's probably going to cause them more trouble in the long run-i.e. medical bills for concussions and legal fees from the various assault charges and tort suits against them.<br /><br />5) I'll be wondering who took care of their dog while they're gone. Those two are the most irresponsible pet owners ever. And they have a cute dog. I always did want a Cairn Terrier.<br /><br />4) Jamie McGuire conveniently forgets that the drinking/gambling age is 21 not 18 and that you're carded for the most part in Vegas.<br /><br />3) Weren't there mob people after Abby and her father in Vegas? Really, that was the best place to get married at. Why not Reno? Seems a little safer to me.<br /><br />2) Because every poor college student can afford to buy a plane ticket at the moment's notice-never mind, ticket prices are a lot more expensive at the last minute.<br /><br />1) I've read this shitty story twice already.</span>
  <a data-text-id="392661050952627561" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer766514870" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16077939496992927460">I read <b>Beautiful Disaster</b> back in 2011 and I remember it being a drama filled, angsty romance that captured my heart and wrung it out! It was an addictive and memorable read and I was thrilled with how things ended. <br/><br/><b>A Beautiful Wedding Novella</b> is meant to fill in some of the gaps we had for Abby and Travis’ wedding. Were there cold feet, or did their intense love for each other stamp out any pre-wedding jitters? All the details of the wedding like where it happened, what they wore, and who knew </span>
  <span id="freeText16077939496992927460" style="display:none">I read <b>Beautiful Disaster</b> back in 2011 and I remember it being a drama filled, angsty romance that captured my heart and wrung it out! It was an addictive and memorable read and I was thrilled with how things ended. <br /><br /><b>A Beautiful Wedding Novella</b> is meant to fill in some of the gaps we had for Abby and Travis’ wedding. Were there cold feet, or did their intense love for each other stamp out any pre-wedding jitters? All the details of the wedding like where it happened, what they wore, and who knew are all filled in with this novella. I was excited to catch up with Abby and Travis and “share” such a joyful occasion. Getting a dual POV is what I wanted in Beautiful Disaster, so I was thrilled to get it here.<br /><br />While I enjoyed some of this novella, parts of it undid the positive feelings I had about their marriage. The way things are left in Beautiful Disaster you’re left to think Abby and Travis getting married impulsively is because they are so crazy in love. And yes, that’s true, but when I got the details of Abby’s thinking and reasoning, it really took away from that gesture. Once again, Abby completely disappointed me while Travis continues to shine. His love and patience for Abby just show how big of a heart he has. Love, love, love Travis since the beginning and my feelings for him have never changed. Unfortunately, I can’t say the same for Abby. I think honesty is the best policy and her reasoning and final actions made my opinion of her even lower than after finishing Walking Disaster.<br /><br />5 stars for Travis, and 1 star for Abby with an overall rating of 3 stars. <br /><i><br />A copy was provided by Atria Books in exchange for an honest review. Thank you! </i></span>
  <a data-text-id="16077939496992927460" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_766222611" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/766222611" />
    <a title="♥Booklish Reviews♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22495428-booklish-reviews"><img alt="♥Booklish Reviews♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1488351025p2/22495428.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/766222611?book_show_action=true">Nov 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥Booklish Reviews♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥Booklish Reviews♥" href="/user/show/22495428-booklish-reviews">♥Booklish Reviews♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22495428-booklish-reviews?shelf=on-the-fence">on-the-fence</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22495428-booklish-reviews?shelf=a-struggle-to-get-through">a-struggle-to-get-through</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22495428-booklish-reviews?shelf=terrible-execution">terrible-execution</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22495428-booklish-reviews?shelf=review-2014">review-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22495428-booklish-reviews?shelf=most-disappointing-2014">most-disappointing-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer766222611" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4510718040748338806"><a href='http://imgur.com/o7WcJx0' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389221239ra/8007253.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/>Before starting this book, I told myself over and over that this was REDEMPTION for McGuire. (Should it turn out to be a good read.)Walking Disaster wasn't up to par. <br/>Friend: A Walking Disaster is amazing! You'll love it. <br/>Me: *AFTER READING*<br/><a href='http://imgur.com/O16ZiZ4' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389221239ra/8007254.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/>There was no redemption for Walking Disaster. This novella was worse than WD. I literally skipped through most of the lengthy paragraphs just to get to the dialogue. It seemed like I was reading filler/previous events that had transpired in Beautiful </span>
  <span id="freeText4510718040748338806" style="display:none"><a href="http://imgur.com/o7WcJx0" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389221239ra/8007253.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Before starting this book, I told myself over and over that this was REDEMPTION for McGuire. (Should it turn out to be a good read.)Walking Disaster wasn't up to par. <br>Friend: A Walking Disaster is amazing! You'll love it. <br>Me: *AFTER READING*<br><a href="http://imgur.com/O16ZiZ4" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389221239ra/8007254.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>There was no redemption for Walking Disaster. This novella was worse than WD. I literally skipped through most of the lengthy paragraphs just to get to the dialogue. It seemed like I was reading filler/previous events that had transpired in Beautiful Diaster. No, we don't need to know that. We've already read it, TWICE, in fact. <br><a href="http://imgur.com/LKfQ5rn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388373773ra/7813511.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>And I'm sorry, but I don't remember Abby cursing this much in BD. She didn't just get a wild hair up her ass and decide to adopt a potty mouth out of nowhere. The different POV's were sometimes hard to tell apart. <br><a href="http://imgur.com/PFN2zDV" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388126449ra/7744345.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>The beginning was so slow. Hell, who am I trying to kid? I was confused throughout the first page. I actually pulled out BD to see if this book would match up with it. I don't like it. In BD Abby acted like she was just soooo in love with Travis that she couldn't go another minute without him. This novella is making it out like she married him because he could possibly go to jail. <br><a href="http://imgur.com/0wI7Tua" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389221239ra/8007255.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>This novella was a complete and total let down. If you value Travis' character and want to keep a decent image of him in your mind, just skip this and move on to something else. <br>Half of this book revolves around Travis and Abby getting out of town and preparing for the wedding. Nothing BIG happens during that. <br>To the editor/agent/publisher of this novella:<br><a href="http://imgur.com/KNVOIFv" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389221239ra/8007256.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>"but it was beautiful, and what we were about to do was beautiful. Even why I was doing it was beautiful..."</i> That was in reference to her wedding dress that she had laid out on the bed.<br><a href="http://imgur.com/dyAI9U0" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389221239ra/8007257.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>And what the hell is up with all of the Bon Jovi references? 1st the quote at the beginning from "Thank You For Loving Me". Then the chapter title for Chapter six...And then the damn discussion in the limo about how Jon Bon Jovi got married in the same chapel (Graceland.)And Travis' mother's note "Thank you for loving my son" ect...<br><a href="http://imgur.com/gm4Obp5" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389221239ra/8007258.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>I don't know, after everything I had read in Beautiful Disaster, and then reading this, when it got to the part where "THING FOR YOU" played at their wedding I rolled my eyes. (This author ruined Travis Maddox for me.)Nothing felt right in this book. <br><a href="http://imgur.com/XkqDsDn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389221239ra/8007259.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>There was no plot in this book, at all. The whole time the reader is left worrying if Travis will go to jail or not and then a year has passed in the story and it's their anniversary. Abby explains that she lied for Travis and he got away with going to jail. (That's pretty much it.) There is no big explanation of how he got away with it, no drama...<br><a href="http://imgur.com/WUHg3u8" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388129178ra/7744874.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>This doesn't even deserve 1 star, but I am going to rate it anyways. This is where Travis Maddox and I separate. He can no longer compete with my other book boyfriend, Lucas. (AKA, "Easy" by Tammara Webber.) <br>I didn't want it to end like this...<br><a href="http://imgur.com/oSsI2SR" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389221239ra/8007260.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>But with so many author's willing to give a new story line and really bust their asses delivering NEW and FRESH material (instead of repeating like McGuire)I just can't continue on with any of her books. This was supposed to be redemption and it wasn't. FAR FROM IT. Money talks and bullshit walks. She ran this series into the ground to where there was virtually nothing left of Travis to love. And it's a damn shame. If you can't give a decent story/plot, don't publish it. Period.<br>And that is how I truly feel after reading this book. I'm done. <br><a href="http://imgur.com/Q5m69bZ" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389221239ra/8007261.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><u>NOVEMBER 2013: THOUGHTS BEFORE THIS BOOK WAS PUBLISHED.</u> <br><br>Another book with Travis Maddox? <br><a href="http://imgur.com/W2rlG8x" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384585795ra/6907689.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>BUT</b> I'll admit I'm a little on-the-fence about this one. Walking Disaster wasn't exactly what I envisioned it to be. I loved Beautiful Disaster, but my love begins and ends there. Walking Disaster was almost the exact same (with a little Travis persona added in) and in the end I was disappointed. So where do I go from here? <br><a href="http://imgur.com/drdQb7J" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384585795ra/6907690.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>I adored Beautiful Disaster and with that comes a loyalty to the author. Some of you might understand what I am saying, others might not. <br>For example: JK Rowling fans adored the Harry Potter series and because of that they marched their happy asses to the store and bought The Casual Vacancy, not knowing what to expect. We go out and buy books from a certain author because of the expectations they set in their previous books. Walking Disaster didn't tickle my fancy. Did I buy it? Yes. Because it was from this author and of course I had expectations. Those expectations weren't met....But I adore Travis' character.<br><a href="http://imgur.com/GFogVd4" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384585795ra/6907691.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>I guess you could say this book would be redemption in a way if it turned out to be good. I could bury the grudge I have with Walking Disaster and have a brighter outlook on McGuire's future novels, which would be ideal in this situation. However, if the book turns out to be terrible...<b> I just don't know</b><br><a href="http://imgur.com/CF5mkti" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384585795ra/6907692.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="4510718040748338806" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_764035250" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/764035250" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/764035250?book_show_action=true">Nov 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781476759555" href="/book/show/18870315-a-beautiful-wedding">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer764035250" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer593712171461287623">All the things we didn't know about Abby & Travis' wedding! <br/><br/><b>
  <u>Likes:</u>
</b><br/><br/>• Travis! How could you not like him? He is sooo sweet and romantic and has definitely grown up!<br/><br/>• My heart went out to Abby even though I didn't like the reasons she wanted to get married, I like that she wanted to protect Travis so fiercely! <br/><br/>• <a href='https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=kwARkjjKHJA<br%20/>' rel='nofollow noopener'>♬ Their song! ♥</a><br/> <br/>• The letter...OMG, definite tearjerker moment!<br/><br/>• The tattoo but the guy was a jerk!<br/><br/>• Sorry America, I liked Vegas better!<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379788875i/515500.jpg' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><b>
  <u>Dislikes:</u>
</b><br/><br/>• Wow, I really didn't like the rea</span>
  <span id="freeText593712171461287623" style="display:none">All the things we didn't know about Abby &amp; Travis' wedding! <br><br><b>
  <u>Likes:</u>
</b><br><br>• Travis! How could you not like him? He is sooo sweet and romantic and has definitely grown up!<br><br>• My heart went out to Abby even though I didn't like the reasons she wanted to get married, I like that she wanted to protect Travis so fiercely! <br><br>• <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=kwARkjjKHJA&lt;br%20/&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">♬ Their song! ♥</a><br> <br>• The letter...OMG, definite tearjerker moment!<br><br>• The tattoo but the guy was a jerk!<br><br>• Sorry America, I liked Vegas better!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379788875i/515500.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>
  <u>Dislikes:</u>
</b><br><br>• Wow, I really didn't like the reasons Abby wanted to get married and that she didn't tell Travis! <br><br>• Not sure if I liked Elvis or not! <br><br>• The quick switch from getting married to the anniversary. A chapter about when they were home would have segued better. <br><br>• The bachelor/bachelorette parties...<i>really?</i> Though I have to admit I would've loved to see you-know-who at Travis'.<br><br>• I didn't really care for the event at St. Thomas - orange and purple? bleh! <br><br><br><b>
  <u>Overall:</u>
</b><br><br>I couldn't NOT read this book even though you can be completely satisfied without reading it. There's just something about Travis that I want to read more of so I'll probably read everything that's written about them ~or~ about the brothers. Yea, I'm ready for those stories! <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388870989i/7948648.jpg" width="400" height="120" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quotes:</u>
</b><br><br>❥ “This is it,” he said. <br><br>“What?” <br><br>“I knew the second I met you that there was something about you I needed. Turns out it wasn’t something about you at all. It was just you.”<br><br>❥ “Uh . . . I was gonna give ’er away.” <br><br>Travis’s mouth pulled to one side. “She was already mine.”<br> <br>❥ "One down, forever to go."<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="593712171461287623" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lisa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lisa" href="/user/show/13978199-lisa">Lisa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=athletes-fighters">athletes-fighters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=paperback-arc">paperback-arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=angsty-romance">angsty-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=arc-given-to-blog-for-honest-review">arc-given-to-blog-for-honest-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=bad-boys">bad-boys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer786873087" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17853778310083167091">*ARC Given to Blog for Honest Review*<br/><br/>Oh boy...<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386900124ra/7476445.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>2 Kisses<br/><br/>I am sad. I am disappointed. I am frustrated beyond all reason. I am confused. I honestly wish I had not read this book and that saddens me to the deepest part of my soul. I <i>almost</i> DNF’d it but my love for Travis and Abby forced me to finish it. I hate that I’m writing all of this stuff, but I have to be honest about my feelings. I am not trying to be rude, insensitive or hurtful at all…these are my thoughts…pure and simple.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386903043ra/7476840.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>The main thing I l</span>
  <span id="freeText17853778310083167091" style="display:none">*ARC Given to Blog for Honest Review*<br><br>Oh boy...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386900124ra/7476445.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>2 Kisses<br><br>I am sad. I am disappointed. I am frustrated beyond all reason. I am confused. I honestly wish I had not read this book and that saddens me to the deepest part of my soul. I <i>almost</i> DNF’d it but my love for Travis and Abby forced me to finish it. I hate that I’m writing all of this stuff, but I have to be honest about my feelings. I am not trying to be rude, insensitive or hurtful at all…these are my thoughts…pure and simple.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386903043ra/7476840.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>The main thing I loved about this book was Travis. He is and always will be one of the best book bf’s ever. He’s amazing! That can never be disputed. The things he would say to Abby just made me melt in a puddle – I <b>love</b> how much he loves her. Travis is worth a million stars in my book. I also loved Travis’s Bachelor Party, especially Trenton’s ‘performance,’ and the little Q&amp;A drinking game at Abby’s Bachelorette party. The other thing I loved…his mom’s letter. <br><br>Okay…let’s get this over with…what didn’t I like. The fact that this book <b>
  <i>
    <u>completely</u>
  </i>
</b> devalues the reason for Abby and Travis getting married. The whole basis for why Abby decides to marry Travis is totally shattered in my heart in one swift clean sentence. That Broke. My. Heart. And the sad thing is…Travis <b>never</b> finds out. <i>Everything</i> after they board that plane to Vegas to me is based on a lie which makes it mean <b>nothing</b>!!! Do you know how much that hurts? I <b>loved</b> the fact that they got married – it was just so them! And now it makes me want to cry. For Travis.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386903043ra/7476841.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The other thing that bugged me…the marriage license. First, it wasn’t being addressed at all, which I thought was a little weird – and then when it was…the way it was being handled was 100% wrong. Am I stickler for details? Well…if I have first hand knowledge of something – then yes, I am going to be a stickler. Call me anal, I’m fine with that. Yes…we read books to escape reality but unless it’s paranormal or fantasy…I expect all the regular laws of the world to still exist. Even though I knew from personal experience what needed to happen, I still Google’d it and I was correct…which makes me even angrier! If I can get an answer within less than 5 minutes…why is there an inaccuracy in the book at all? I don’t understand.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380419032ra/830288.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The writing was not cutting it for me either…it was long winded, overly and unnecessarily descriptive at times, there were point it dragged and I was tempted to skim and there was even one typo! And a pretty obvious and bad one too – when you call America, American , I’m going to raise an eyebrow. In over 700 combined pages of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/446537565" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <i>Beautiful Disaster</i>
</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/446705580" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <i>Walking Disaster</i>
</a> that didn’t happen <b>once</b> (at least not that I caught) but it did in a 160 page novella. I do not remember any of this happening at all with <i>BD</i> and <i>WD</i>…or maybe because of the things that I was already frustrated with, all the little things that I could normally or possibly overlook started to stand out more. Who knows…<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386526644ra/7384003.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I think the other thing that really got me was during <i>BD</i> and <i>WD</i> I never questioned any part of Travis and Abby’s relationship. In the moment, it was all there for me – the emotions and feelings, I just got them. <i>That’s</i> what happens to me when I <b>truly</b> feel it…I don’t care if logic should tell me that it’s too soon or too fast…if I believe what the characters are feeling, then I’m sold. There were parts of <i>Beautiful Wedding</i> that made me question things. Mainly because of stuff Abby was saying! So on top of hating that their wedding is based on a lie, now I’m questioning their relationship as well. <i>Dude</i>! That sucks!<br><br>I hate regrets…but regretting that I read a book, this is a new and awful experience for me. One I hope to never experience again.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434116i/874066.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434116i/874067.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="17853778310083167091" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer13453910105209934208"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395426i/761624._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>♥♥♥ 3.5 'Beautiful Wedding' Stars ♥♥♥</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386734445ra/7431321.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>"The only thing I'm afraid of is a life without you, Pigeon."<br/><br/>"Then you have nothing to be afraid of," I said. "We're forever."<br/><br/>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg' width='405' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This was such a sweet novella. The story starts off pretty much when Abby proposes to Travis and what happened in Vegas. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386734061ra/7431158.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>“She told me to find a girl worth fighting for. The o</b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText13453910105209934208" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395426i/761624._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>♥♥♥ 3.5 'Beautiful Wedding' Stars ♥♥♥</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386734445ra/7431321.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"The only thing I'm afraid of is a life without you, Pigeon."<br><br>"Then you have nothing to be afraid of," I said. "We're forever."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was such a sweet novella. The story starts off pretty much when Abby proposes to Travis and what happened in Vegas. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386734061ra/7431158.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“She told me to find a girl worth fighting for. The one that doesn't come easy. She said to never stop fighting and I didn't. She was right."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>But I have got to say... I was SO DAMN frustrated by Abby. Her reasons for this wedding just made me upset for Travis. I mean... COME ON!! I would be jumping for joy to be marrying Travis because he is just the BEST! And there are many reasons why you would want to be with him. But anyways, like I said before, I didn't like <i>her</i> reason for doing it.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384206818ra/6813918.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"I saw pictures of my parents' wedding. I thought Mom was the most beautiful bride I'd ever see. Then I saw you at the Chapel, and I changed my mind."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>Travis, still love him to pieces!! *sigh* I can never dislike him. He was so ADORABLE, and LOVING, and CARING, and SEXY... just AWESOME. I think he was so thoughtful and was so committed to Abby, something I felt Abby lacked in the beginning. But Travis was just amazing!! I LOVED him!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386734547ra/7431373.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"You were right," I said. Travis pulled back to look at me, curious. "You were my last first kiss."<br><br>He was breathing heavily but still managed to sweetly whisper, "I fucking love you, Pigeon."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>There were many sweet moments. I teared up a bit in one part in particular. And there was one part that had me laughing out loud. It was really good. Story wise, this novella doesn't add to it, because we all know how this ends for them, but we finally get to see how it all went down. I really enjoyed it. I was so happy for them and the last part of the book was the best. I loved Travis! I liked the interactions with their family and friends. I just Really liked it!! If you loved Beautiful Disaster, then you can't miss out on this novella. Even if Abby is annoying.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1887387461592634920"><b>
  <i>“A Maddox boy will take you all the way to the edge, but if you go with him, he’ll follow you anywhere.”<br/><br/>“He will love you with everything he has for as long as you let him.” </i>
</b><br/><br/>I am a mad fan of anything featuring Travis Maddox , and although I was a little apprehensive about reading this – not wanting it to ruin the utter, utter perfection of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11505797.Beautiful_Disaster__Beautiful___1_' title='Beautiful Disaster (Beautiful, #1) by Jamie McGuire' rel='nofollow noopener'>Beautiful Disaster</a> – it turns out I’m just way to obsessed with my #1 bad boy to stay away. <br/><br/>If you haven’t read <i>Beautiful Disaster</i>, this is going to be a</span>
  <span id="freeText1887387461592634920" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>“A Maddox boy will take you all the way to the edge, but if you go with him, he’ll follow you anywhere.”<br /><br />“He will love you with everything he has for as long as you let him.” </i>
</b><br /><br />I am a mad fan of anything featuring Travis Maddox , and although I was a little apprehensive about reading this – not wanting it to ruin the utter, utter perfection of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11505797.Beautiful_Disaster__Beautiful___1_" title="Beautiful Disaster (Beautiful, #1) by Jamie McGuire" rel="nofollow noopener">Beautiful Disaster</a> – it turns out I’m just way to obsessed with my #1 bad boy to stay away. <br /><br />If you haven’t read <i>Beautiful Disaster</i>, this is going to be a little spoilery, so I calmly suggest that you turn away from this review, put down whatever book you are reading now, go and buy it and start immediately!!<br /><br />This book picks up at the scene where Abby proposes to Travis, and not only do we get the absolute bonus of having dual POV (WIN!), but we also get to see a little further into Abby’s thought processes and I've gotta say, I was pissed with her... AGAIN! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I’m really disappointed that THAT was the reason why she proposed, and my heart broke for poor Travis that that was what she was thinking, and she initially wasn't fully committed. Although she (almost fully) redeemed herself later on, I’m yet again disappointed with Abby and her stupid lies, and the fact that she is still keeping things from Travis. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br /><br />Of course Travis is absolute perfection. He is so crazy in love with his Pidge, and so happy and excited to be marrying her. You can feel his devotion to her and his passion for her, and he just proves once again what makes him so incredibly special. I read most of the novella with a huge grin on my face just soaking up his joy. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“My God, that woman was fucking sexy. She didn’t even have to try, and all I wanted was to be all up in her business. Now that we were engaged that didn’t sound like such a bastard thing to think.”<br /><br />“I’m probably not going to make sense for the next six months while I try to process the fact that I’ve gotten everything I’ve ever wanted.”</i>
</blockquote><br />Taking us beyond the end of <i>Beautiful Disaster</i>, we get to see a little bit into the future, and even though it was brief, I loved the glimpse we got of Travis and Abby living their lives together still madly in love and blissfully happy.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Travis Maddox loved me in a way most people dreamed about.”</i>
</blockquote><br />Featuring many beautifully swoony moments, an Elvis impersonator, one hot wedding night, a tear-inducing letter and one scary as all hell stripper, despite my early annoyance, I thought this was a great finish to Travis and Abby’s story. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“I want you to know that whatever love is, this has got to be it. We were best friends first, and we tried not to fall in love, and we did anyway. If you’re not with me, it’s not where I want to be. I’m in this. I’m with you.”</i>
</blockquote><br />4 ‘I LOVE TRAVIS’ stars.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1887387461592634920" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
